/*Drop tables*/
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS pokemon_paste;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS move;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS move_cat;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS gender;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS item;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS pkmn_ability;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ability;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS nature;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS pokemon_type_combination;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS pokemon_type;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS pokemon;

/*Table creation*/

CREATE TABLE pokemon (
    id INT(4) AUTO_INCREMENT NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(60) NOT NULL,
    hp INT(3) NOT NULL,
    atk INT(3) NOT NULL,
    def INT(3) NOT NULL,
    spatk INT(3) NOT NULL,
    spdef INT(3) NOT NULL,
    spd INT(3) NOT NULL,
    bst INT(3) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_pokemon PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

CREATE TABLE pokemon_type (
    id INT(2) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_pokemon_type PRIMARY KEY (id)
); 

CREATE TABLE pokemon_type_combination (
    id_pokemon INT(4) NOT NULL,
    id_type INT(2) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_pokemon_type_combination PRIMARY KEY (id_pokemon, id_type),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_type_combination_pokemon FOREIGN KEY (id_pokemon) REFERENCES pokemon(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_type_combination_type FOREIGN KEY (id_type) REFERENCES pokemon_type(id)
);

CREATE TABLE nature (
    id INT(2) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_nature PRIMARY KEY (id)
); 

CREATE TABLE ability (
    id INT(3) AUTO_INCREMENT NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
    description VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_ability PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

CREATE TABLE pkmn_ability (
    id_pokemon INT(4) NOT NULL,
    id_ability INT(3) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_pkmn_ability PRIMARY KEY (id_pokemon, id_ability),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pkmn_ability_pokemon FOREIGN KEY (id_pokemon) REFERENCES pokemon(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pkmn_ability_ability FOREIGN KEY (id_ability) REFERENCES ability(id)
);

CREATE TABLE item (
    id INT(3) AUTO_INCREMENT NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(50),
    description VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_item PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

CREATE TABLE gender (
    id INT(2) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_gender PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

CREATE TABLE move_cat (
    id INT(1) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_move_cat PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

CREATE TABLE move (
    id INT(3) AUTO_INCREMENT NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    id_type INT(2) NOT NULL,
    id_move_cat INT(1), 
    power INT(3),
    accuracy INT(3),
    pp INT(3),
    effect VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    effect_prob int(3),
    CONSTRAINT pk_move PRIMARY KEY (id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_move_type FOREIGN KEY (id_type) REFERENCES pokemon_type(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_move_cat FOREIGN KEY (id_move_cat) REFERENCES move_cat(id)
);

CREATE TABLE pokemon_paste (
    id INT(4) AUTO_INCREMENT NOT NULL,
    id_pokemon INT(4) NOT NULL,
    id_item INT(3),
    nickname VARCHAR(18),
    level INT(3) DEFAULT 100 NOT NULL,
    id_gender INT(2),
    is_shiny BOOLEAN,
    id_tera_type INT(2) NOT NULL,
    id_ability INT(3) NOT NULL,
    move1 INT(3),
    move2 INT(3),
    move3 INT(3),
    move4 INT(3),
    hp_ev INT(3) DEFAULT 0,
    atk_ev INT(3) DEFAULT 0,
    def_ev INT(3) DEFAULT 0,
    spatk_ev INT(3) DEFAULT 0,
    spdef_ev INT(3) DEFAULT 0,
    spd_ev INT(3) DEFAULT 0,
    hp_iv INT(3) DEFAULT 31,
    atk_iv INT(3) DEFAULT 31,
    def_iv INT(3) DEFAULT 31,
    spatk_iv INT(3) DEFAULT 31,
    spdef_iv INT(3) DEFAULT 31,
    spd_iv INT(3) DEFAULT 31,
    hp INT(3),
    atk INT(3),
    def INT(3),
    spatk INT(3),
    spdef INT(3),
    spd INT(3),
    id_nature INT(2) DEFAULT 13 NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT pk_pokemon_paste PRIMARY KEY (id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_pokemon FOREIGN KEY (id_pokemon) REFERENCES pokemon(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_ability FOREIGN KEY (id_ability) REFERENCES ability(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_item FOREIGN KEY (id_item) REFERENCES item(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_gender FOREIGN KEY (id_gender) REFERENCES gender(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_tera FOREIGN KEY (id_tera_type) REFERENCES pokemon_type(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_move1 FOREIGN KEY (move1) REFERENCES move(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_move2 FOREIGN KEY (move2) REFERENCES move(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_move3 FOREIGN KEY (move3) REFERENCES move(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_move4 FOREIGN KEY (move4) REFERENCES move(id),
    CONSTRAINT fk_pokemon_paste_nature FOREIGN KEY (id_nature) REFERENCES nature(id)
);
